href=\"http://blogs.ubc.ca/christinahendricks/\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://blogs.ubc.ca/christinahendricks/', 'Christina Hendricks']);\" target=\"_blank\" textbook” for introductory courses in philosophy. It originally appeared on her blog,&nbsp;<em><a href=\"http://blogs.ubc.ca/chendricks/\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://blogs.ubc.ca/chendricks/', 'You’re The Teacher']);\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">You’re The Teacher</a></em>.</p>\n<p> <a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/20/open-textbook-introduction-philosophy-guest-post-christina-hendricks/\" class=\"more-link\">(more…)</a></p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__date\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-time\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\"><abbr class=\"published updated\" title=\"2017-04-20T08:56:18+00:00\">April 20, 2017</abbr></span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__comments\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/20/open-textbook-introduction-philosophy-guest-post-christina-hendricks/#comments\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-comment\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t2 \t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__likes\">\n\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-heart\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t10\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t</footer>\t</article>\n<article class=\"mosaic__item article-archive article-archive--masonry no-thumbnail post-16197 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-public-philosophy-and-outreach tag-choices tag-errol-morris tag-past tag-philosophy tag-thomas-kuhn\" style=\"position: absolute; Among those interviewed for the episode is acclaimed filmmaker <a href=\"http://errolmorris.com/\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://errolmorris.com/', 'Errol Morris']);\" target=\"_blank\">Errol Morris</a>, and he has some interesting things to say about Thomas Kuhn. <a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/20/errol-morris-vs-thomas-kuhn/\" class=\"more-link\">(more…)</a></p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__date\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-time\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\"><abbr class=\"published updated\" title=\"2017-04-20T01:12:13+00:00\">April 20, 2017</abbr></span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__comments\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/20/errol-morris-vs-thomas-kuhn/#comments\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-comment\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t4 \t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__likes\">\n\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-heart\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t5\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t</footer>\t</article>\n<article class=\"mosaic__item article-archive article-archive--masonry no-thumbnail post-16194 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-awards-grants-honors tag-award tag-berggruen tag-philosophy tag-prize\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 627px;\">\n\t\t\t\n<header class=\"article__header\">\n\t\t\t<h3 class=\"article__title entry-title\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/nominations-open-1-million-prize-philosophers/\" rel=\"bookmark\">Nominations Open For $1 Million Prize, Now Not Just For Philosophers</a>\n\t\t</h3>\n\t\t<span class=\"vcard author\"><span class=\"fn\"><span class=\"value-title\" title=\"Justin W.\"></span></span></span>\n</header>\t\t<section class=\"article__content entry-summary\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/nominations-open-1-million-prize-philosophers/\">\n\t\t\t\t</a><p><a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/nominations-open-1-million-prize-philosophers/\">The Berggruen Institute has begun soliciting </a><a href=\"http://berggruen.org/nominations\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://berggruen.org/nominations', 'nominations']);\" target=\"_blank\">nominations</a> for the second winner of its $1 million “<a href=\"http://philosophyandculture.berggruen.org/councils/the-berggruen-prize\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://philosophyandculture.berggruen.org/councils/the-berggruen-prize', 'Berggruen Prize']);\" target=\"_blank\">Berggruen Prize</a>.” The <a href=\"http://dailynous.com/2016/10/04/charles-taylor-wins-million-dollar-berggruen-prize/\">inaugural winner was Charles Taylor</a>. Who should win it this time around? <a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/nominations-open-1-million-prize-philosophers/\" class=\"more-link\">(more…)</a></p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__date\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-time\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\"><abbr class=\"published updated\" title=\"2017-04-19T13:50:17+00:00\">April 19, 2017</abbr></span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__comments\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/nominations-open-1-million-prize-philosophers/#comments\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-comment\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t6 \t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__likes\">\n\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-heart\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t0\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t</footer>\t</article>\n<article class=\"mosaic__item article-archive article-archive--masonry no-thumbnail post-16185 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-teaching-2 tag-philosophy-major tag-popularity\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 816px;\">\n\t\t\t\n<header class=\"article__header\">\n\t\t\t<h3 class=\"article__title entry-title\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/philosophy-really-89th-popular-major/\" rel=\"bookmark\">Is Philosophy Really The 89th Most Popular Major? Update: No</a>\n\t\t</h3>\n\t\t<span class=\"vcard author\"><span class=\"fn\"><span class=\"value-title\" title=\"Justin W.\"></span></span></span>\n</header>\t\t<section class=\"article__content entry-summary\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/philosophy-really-89th-popular-major/\">\n\t\t\t\t</a><p><a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/philosophy-really-89th-popular-major/\">A site called </a><a href=\"http://www.matchcollege.com/top-majors\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.matchcollege.com/top-majors', 'Match College']);\" target=\"_blank\">Match College</a> lists philosophy as the 89th most popular major. It comes in just after “Baking and Pastry” and “Respiratory Therapy,” which is perfect, because if true I will need to take some deep breaths and console myself with a piece of cake. <a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/19/philosophy-really-89th-popular-major/\" class=\"more-link\">(more…)</a></p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"article__title entry-title\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/when-to-turn-it-off/\" rel=\"bookmark\">When To Turn It Off</a>\n\t\t</h3>\n\t\t<span class=\"vcard author\"><span class=\"fn\"><span class=\"value-title\" title=\"Justin W.\"></span></span></span>\n</header>\t\t<section class=\"article__content entry-summary\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/when-to-turn-it-off/\">\n\t\t\t\t<p><em>Here’s a… hypothesis for why many habits of philosophical thinking might not come naturally. The hypothesis is that some tools for critical evaluation run counter to another valuable set of tools: our tools for effective social engagement. These tools help us make sense of what someone is saying by encouraging us to interpret underspecified claims in the most posi..</em></p>\n\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__date\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-time\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\"><abbr class=\"published updated\" title=\"2017-04-10T11:06:25+00:00\">April 10, 2017</abbr></span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__comments\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/when-to-turn-it-off/#comments\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-comment\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t10 \t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__likes\">\n\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-heart\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t3\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t</footer>\t</article>\n<article class=\"mosaic__item article-archive article-archive--masonry no-thumbnail post-16064 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-news-2 tag-abducted tag-academic-freedom tag-missing tag-philosopher tag-turkey\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 5262px;\">\n\t\t\t\n<header class=\"article__header\">\n\t\t\t<h3 class=\"article__title entry-title\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/philosophy-instructor-reportedly-abducted/\" rel=\"bookmark\">Philosophy Instructor Reportedly Abducted</a>\n\t\t</h3>\n\t\t<span class=\"vcard author\"><span class=\"fn\"><span class=\"value-title\" title=\"Justin W.\"></span></span></span>\n</header>\t\t<section class=\"article__content entry-summary\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/philosophy-instructor-reportedly-abducted/\">\n\t\t\t\t</a><p><a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/philosophy-instructor-reportedly-abducted/\">Önder Asan, a philosophy instructor from Ankara, Turkey, was </a><a href=\"https://turkeypurge.com/second-alleged-disappearance-in-a-week-philosophy-teacher-goes-missing\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'https://turkeypurge.com/second-alleged-disappearance-in-a-week-philosophy-teacher-goes-missing', 'reportedly abducted']);\" target=\"_blank\">reportedly abducted</a> there on April 1st. Asan had worked at one of the educational institutions* closed down by the Turkish government following the attempted military coup there last July. <a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/philosophy-instructor-reportedly-abducted/\" class=\"more-link\">(more…)</a></p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</section>\n\t\t<footer class=\"article__meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__date\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-time\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\"><abbr class=\"published updated\" title=\"2017-04-10T10:10:40+00:00\">April 10, 2017</abbr></span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__comments\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://dailynous.com/2017/04/10/philosophy-instructor-reportedly-abducted/#respond\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-comment\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t0\t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-box  article__likes\">\n\t\t\t\t<i class=\"icon-heart\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"meta-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t1\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t</footer>\t</article>\n<article class=\"mosaic__item article-archive article-archive--masonry no-thumbnail post-16060 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-awards-grants-honors tag-essay-prize tag-journal tag-mind tag-philosophy\" style=\"position: absolute;
